         FROM [sys].[extended_properties] AS [ep]

             AND [ep].[minor_id] = 0
             AND [ep].[class] = 1
             AND [ep].[name] = N'microsoft_database_tools_support'
    )
)
SELECT 1 ELSE SELECT 0

SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[CreatedAt], [m].[Description], [m].[IsActive], [m].[Name], [m1].[Id], [m1].[CreatedAt], [m1].[Description], [m1].[ImageUrl], [m1].[IsAvailable], [m1].[MenuId], [m1].[Name], [m1].[Price]
FROM [Menus] AS [m]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [m0].[Id], [m0].[CreatedAt], [m0].[Description], [m0].[ImageUrl], [m0].[IsAvailable], [m0].[MenuId], [m0].[Name], [m0].[Price]

) AS [m1] ON [m].[Id] = [m1].[MenuId]

ORDER BY [m].[Name], [m].[Id]
